YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 140-rules system (140 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 140-rules system (140 strict rules).
Removing 140 relatively RFC-match-bounded rules [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, WST 2022].
Remains to prove termination of a 0-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED
